	<ul style="list-style-type:circle">
		<li>-0.0 points from 4.9% during 2018. </em>(not statistically significant)</em></li>
		<li>0.4 points from 4.4% during 2014. </em>(statistically significant)</em></li>

	</li>
</ul>
